"code": 'import requests\nimport os\nfrom langchain_community.document_loaders import PyPDFLoader\nimport json\nfrom datetime import datetime\nimport tempfile\n\nprint(\'=== DOWNLOADING AND ANALYZING TOP JUNE 2022 AI REGULATION PAPERS ===\')\nprint(\'Objective: Download priority papers and search for figures with three axes\')\nprint(\'Focus: Find figures with label words at both ends of each axis\\n\')\n\n# First, let\'s inspect the analysis file to understand the structure\nanalysis_file = \'workspace/june_2022_papers_analysis.json\'\n\nif not os.path.exists(analysis_file):\n print(f\'Error: Analysis file not found: {analysis_file}\')\nelse:\n print(\'Step 1: Inspecting analysis file structure...\')\n \n with open(analysis_file, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n analysis_data = json.load(f)\n \n print(f\'Analysis data keys: {list(analysis_data.keys())}\')\n \n # Check the structure of priority papers\n if \'priority_papers_for_download\' in analysis_data:\n priority_papers = analysis_data[\'priority_papers_for_download\']\n print(f\'Number of priority papers: {len(priority_papers)}\')\n \n if priority_papers:\n print(f\'First paper structure: {list(priority_papers[0].keys())}\')\n else:\n print(\'No priority papers found in analysis data\')\n priority_papers = []\n \n print(\'\\n=== STEP 2: DOWNLOADING TOP PRIORITY PAPERS ===\')\n \n downloaded_papers = []\n \n # Start with the top 3 priority papers to avoid overwhelming the system\n top_papers = priority_papers[:3]\n \n for i, paper in enumerate(top_papers, 1):\n title = paper.get(\'title\', \'Unknown Title\')\n arxiv_id = paper.get(\'arxiv_id\', \'Unknown ID\')\n pdf_link = paper.get(\'pdf_link\', \'\')\n \n print(f\'\\n--- DOWNLOADING PAPER {i}/3 ---\')\n print(f\'Title: {title}\')\n print(f\'arXiv ID: {arxiv_id}\')\n print(f\'PDF Link: {pdf_link}\')\n \n if not pdf_link:\n print(\'No PDF link available, skipping...\')\n continue\n \n try:\n # Set up headers to mimic a browser request\n headers = {\n \'User-Agent\': \'Mozilla/5.0 (Windows NT 10.0; Win64; x64) AppleWebKit/537.36 (KHTML, like Gecko) Chrome/91.0.4472.124 Safari/537.36\',\n \'Accept\': \'application/pdf,application/octet-stream,*/*\',\n \'Accept-Language\': \'en-US,en;q=0.9\',\n \'Connection\': \'keep-alive\'\n }\n \n print(\'Making request to download PDF...\')\n response = requests.get(pdf_link, headers=headers, timeout=60, stream=True)\n \n print(f\'Response status: {response.status_code}\')\n print(f\'Content type: {response.headers.get("Content-Type", "unknown")}\')\n \n if response.status_code == 200:\n # Save the PDF to workspace\n safe_filename = f\'paper_{i}_{arxiv_id.replace("/", "_").replace(".", "_")}.pdf\'\n pdf_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', safe_filename)\n \n with open(pdf_path, \'wb\') as pdf_file:\n for chunk in response.iter_content(chunk_size=8192):\n if chunk:\n pdf_file.write(chunk)\n \n file_size = os.path.getsize(pdf_path)\n print(f\'‚úì PDF downloaded successfully: {safe_filename} ({file_size:,} bytes)\')\n \n # Verify the file is a valid PDF by checking file size and headers\n if file_size > 1000: # Minimum reasonable PDF size\n downloaded_papers.append({\n \'title\': title,\n \'arxiv_id\': arxiv_id,\n \'pdf_path\': pdf_path,\n \'file_size\': file_size,\n \'original_link\': pdf_link\n })\n print(\'‚úì Paper added to analysis queue\')\n else:\n print(\'‚ö† PDF file seems too small, may be invalid\')\n os.remove(pdf_path)\n \n else:\n print(f\'Failed to download PDF: HTTP {response.status_code}\')\n print(f\'Response content preview: {response.text[:200]}...\')\n \n except Exception as e:\n print(f\'Error downloading paper {i}: {str(e)}\')\n continue\n \n print(f\'\\n=== STEP 3: PARSING DOWNLOADED PAPERS FOR FIGURES ===\')\n print(f\'Successfully downloaded papers: {len(downloaded_papers)}\')\n \n figures_analysis = []\n \n for i, paper in enumerate(downloaded_papers, 1):\n print(f\'\\n--- ANALYZING PAPER {i}: {paper["title"][:50]}... ---\')\n print(f\'File: {paper["pdf_path"]} ({paper["file_size"]:,} bytes)\')\n \n try:\n # Use PyPDFLoader to extract text from the PDF\n print(\'Extracting text from PDF...\')\n loader = PyPDFLoader(paper[\'pdf_path\'])\n pages = loader.load_and_split()\n \n print(f\'PDF successfully parsed: {len(pages)} pages\')\n \n # Combine all text content\n full_text = \'\\n\'.join([page.page_content for page in pages])\n print(f\'Total text length: {len(full_text):,} characters\')\n \n # Search for figure-related content and axis mentions\n text_lower = full_text.lower()\n \n # Keywords that might indicate figures with axes\n figure_keywords = [\'figure\', \'fig.\', \'chart\', \'graph\', \'plot\', \'diagram\']\n axis_keywords = [\'axis\', \'axes\', \'x-axis\', \'y-axis\', \'z-axis\', \'horizontal\', \'vertical\']\n three_axis_keywords = [\'three\', \'3\', \'three-dimensional\', \'3d\', \'three axes\', \'three axis\']\n \n # Count occurrences of relevant keywords\n figure_mentions = sum(text_lower.count(keyword) for keyword in figure_keywords)\n axis_mentions = sum(text_lower.count(keyword) for keyword in axis_keywords)\n three_axis_mentions = sum(text_lower.count(keyword) for keyword in three_axis_keywords)\n \n print(f\'Figure-related mentions: {figure_mentions}\')\n print(f\'Axis-related mentions: {axis_mentions}\')\n print(f\'Three-axis mentions: {three_axis_mentions}\')\n \n # Look for specific patterns that might indicate three-axis figures\n potential_figure_contexts = []\n \n # Search for contexts around figure mentions\n import re\n figure_pattern = r\'(figure\\s+\\d+|fig\\.\\s*\\d+)\'\n figure_matches = re.finditer(figure_pattern, text_lower)\n \n for match in figure_matches:\n start_pos = max(0, match.start() - 200)\n end_pos = min(len(full_text), match.end() + 300)\n context = full_text[start_pos:end_pos]\n \n # Check if this context mentions axes or dimensions\n context_lower = context.lower()\n if any(keyword in context_lower for keyword in axis_keywords + three_axis_keywords):\n potential_figure_contexts.append({\n \'figure_reference\': match.group(),\n \'context\': context,\n \'position\': match.start()\n })\n \n print(f\'Potential figure contexts found: {len(potential_figure_contexts)}\')\n \n # Display the most promising contexts\n if potential_figure_contexts:\n print(\'\\n*** PROMISING FIGURE CONTEXTS ***\')\n for j, context_info in enumerate(potential_figure_contexts[:3], 1):\n print(f\'\\nContext {j} - {context_info["figure_reference"]}:\')\n print(f\'{context_info["context"]}\')\n print(\'-\' * 60)\n \n # Look for specific patterns that might indicate label words at axis ends\n label_patterns = [\n r\'\\b(low|high)\\b.*\\b(low|high)\\b\', # Common axis end labels\n r\'\\b(left|right)\\b.*\\b(top|bottom)\\b\',\n r\'\\b(positive|negative)\\b.*\\b(positive|negative)\\b\',\n r\'\\b(minimum|maximum)\\b.*\\b(minimum|maximum)\\b\'\n ]\n \n label_contexts = []\n for pattern in label_patterns:\n matches = re.finditer(pattern, text_lower)\n for match in matches:\n start_pos = max(0, match.start() - 150)\n end_pos = min(len(full_text), match.end() + 150)\n context = full_text[start_pos:end_pos]\n label_contexts.append({\n \'pattern\': pattern,\n \'match\': match.group(),\n \'context\': context\n })\n \n if label_contexts:\n print(\'\\n*** POTENTIAL AXIS LABEL CONTEXTS ***\')\n for j, label_info in enumerate(label_contexts[:2], 1):\n print(f\'\\nLabel Context {j}:\')\n print(f\'Match: {label_info["match"]}\')\n print(f\'Context: {label_info["context"]}\')\n print(\'-\' * 60)\n \n # Save analysis for this paper\n paper_analysis = {\n \'paper_title\': paper[\'title\'],\n \'arxiv_id\': paper[\'arxiv_id\'],\n \'pdf_path\': paper[\'pdf_path\'],\n \'pages_count\': len(pages),\n \'text_length\': len(full_text),\n \'figure_mentions\': figure_mentions,\n \'axis_mentions\': axis_mentions,\n \'three_axis_mentions\': three_axis_mentions,\n \'potential_figure_contexts\': len(potential_figure_contexts),\n \'potential_label_contexts\': len(label_contexts),\n \'figure_contexts_sample\': potential_figure_contexts[:3],\n \'label_contexts_sample\': label_contexts[:2],\n \'analysis_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n }\n \n figures_analysis.append(paper_analysis)\n \n # Save the full text for manual inspection if needed\n text_file = paper[\'pdf_path\'].replace(\'.pdf\', \'_text.txt\')\n with open(text_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n f.write(full_text)\n print(f\'‚úì Full text saved to: {os.path.basename(text_file)}\')\n \n except Exception as e:\n print(f\'Error analyzing paper {i}: {str(e)}\')\n continue\n \n # Save comprehensive analysis results\n analysis_results = {\n \'analysis_timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat(),\n \'papers_downloaded\': len(downloaded_papers),\n \'papers_analyzed\': len(figures_analysis),\n \'objective\': \'Find figures with three axes containing label words at both ends\',\n \'downloaded_papers\': downloaded_papers,\n \'figures_analysis\': figures_analysis,\n \'summary\': {\n \'total_figure_mentions\': sum(paper.get(\'figure_mentions\', 0) for paper in figures_analysis),\n \'total_axis_mentions\': sum(paper.get(\'axis_mentions\', 0) for paper in figures_analysis),\n \'total_three_axis_mentions\': sum(paper.get(\'three_axis_mentions\', 0) for paper in figures_analysis),\n \'papers_with_figure_contexts\': sum(1 for paper in figures_analysis if paper.get(\'potential_figure_contexts\', 0) > 0)\n }\n }\n \n results_file = \'workspace/papers_figures_analysis.json\'\n with open(results_file, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n json.dump(analysis_results, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n \n print(f\'\\n=== ANALYSIS COMPLETE ===\')\n print(f\'Papers downloaded and analyzed: {len(figures_analysis)}\')\n print(f\'Analysis results saved to: {os.path.basename(results_file)}\')\n \n # Summary of findings\n if figures_analysis:\n print(f\'\\n=== SUMMARY OF FINDINGS ===\')\n total_figures = sum(paper.get(\'figure_mentions\', 0) for paper in figures_analysis)\n total_axes = sum(paper.get(\'axis_mentions\', 0) for paper in figures_analysis)\n papers_with_contexts = sum(1 for paper in figures_analysis if paper.get(\'potential_figure_contexts\', 0) > 0)\n \n print(f\'Total figure mentions across all papers: {total_figures}\')\n print(f\'Total axis mentions across all papers: {total_axes}\')\n print(f\'Papers with promising figure contexts: {papers_with_contexts}\')\n \n # Identify the most promising paper\n if figures_analysis:\n best_paper = max(figures_analysis, key=lambda p: (\n p.get(\'three_axis_mentions\', 0) * 3 + \n p.get(\'potential_figure_contexts\', 0) * 2 + \n p.get(\'axis_mentions\', 0)\n ))\n \n print(f\'\\n*** MOST PROMISING PAPER ***\')\n print(f\'Title: {best_paper["paper_title"]}\')\n print(f\'arXiv ID: {best_paper["arxiv_id"]}\')\n print(f\'Figure mentions: {best_paper.get("figure_mentions", 0)}\')\n print(f\'Axis mentions: {best_paper.get("axis_mentions", 0)}\')\n print(f\'Three-axis mentions: {best_paper.get("three_axis_mentions", 0)}\')\n print(f\'Figure contexts found: {best_paper.get("potential_figure_contexts", 0)}\')\n \n print(f\'\\nFiles created in workspace:\')\n for file in sorted(os.listdir(\'workspace\')):\n if file.endswith((\'.pdf\', \'.txt\', \'.json\')):\n file_path = os.path.join(\'workspace\', file)\n file_size = os.path.getsize(file_path)\n print(f\' - {file} ({file_size:,} bytes)\')',
